CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>insert into ingredient (id, name, category, price) values (1, 'tomato', 'vegetable', 0.99);</s>
